<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Corning is one of the world's leading innovators in materials science, with a 170+ year track record of life-changing inventions. Corning applies its unparalleled expertise in glass science, ceramics science, and optical physics along with its deep manufacturing and engineering capabilities to develop category-defining products that transform industries and enhance people's lives. Corning succeeds through sustained investment in RD&amp;E, a unique combination of material and process innovation, and deep, trust-based relationships with customers who are global leaders in their industries. 

Corning's capabilities are versatile and synergistic, which allows the company to evolve to meet changing market needs, while also helping our customers capture new opportunities in dynamic industries. Today, Corning's markets include optical communications, mobile consumer electronics, display technology, automotive, and life sciences vessels. Corning's industry-leading products include damage-resistant cover glass for mobile devices; precision glass for advanced displays; optical fiber, wireless technologies, and connectivity solutions for state-of-the-art communications networks; trusted products to accelerate drug discovery and delivery; and clean-air technologies for cars and trucks.

Terms of Use: http://ow.ly/ObPiI
          </p>

<!---->    </div>
  

      </div>
  
        
      </div>

      
            
            
  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We’re collaborating with <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/microsoft?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Microsoft</a> Azure to redefine fiber networks. 

Corning will manufacture Microsoft’s Hollow Core Fiber in North Carolina, boosting the speed and reliability of Azure’s global network. The future of <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fai&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AI</a> and Cloud connectivity is here. Learn more from <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/corning-cable-systems/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Corning Optical Communications</a>' Signal Blog: <a class="link" href="http://ms.spr.ly/6041sSGdX?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>http://ms.spr.ly/6041sSGdX</a>.  </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">In Harrodsburg, KY, Corning isn’t just a workplace, it’s a part of the community’s fabric. Generations of families have built their lives around the opportunities created here. 

Apple’s continued investment into this small-town is not only making a global impact, contributing to devices used around the world but an impact within a community. A community that feels the advancement is about more than just innovation, but also one of legacy, families, and a brighter future for the next generation. <a class="link" href="http://ms.spr.ly/6047sW2FU?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>http://ms.spr.ly/6047sW2FU</a>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Chairman and CEO, Wendell Weeks, and Apple CEO, Tim Cook, sat down with Jim Cramer live from our Harrodsburg, Kentucky facility on last night’s episode of <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/cnbc?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>CNBC</a>’s Mad Money. During the discussion, they shared how Corning and Apple are driving U.S. advanced manufacturing and creating a lasting community impact in Kentucky.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We’re honored to be recognized among <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/newsweek?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Newsweek</a>'s list of the World’s Most Trustworthy Companies for 2025! 

This prestigious recognition reflects feedback from 65,000 people across 20 countries, who evaluated companies on three key dimensions of customer trust, employee trust, and investor trust. Here’s to continuing to earn and build trust as a leading innovator in materials science. <a class="link" href="http://ms.spr.ly/6046sibdG?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>http://ms.spr.ly/6046sibdG</a> </p>
